OMXH Shortlist – full table : generated 2025-11-18 10:33 UTC

LEGEND / HOW TO READ
- Edge v6 = all formulas (blended).
- Edge v4 = base formulas.
- Edge (NoVol) = without volume factors.
- Prob Up (Anchor) = anchor model probability.
- P(Up) Mkv1 / Mkv2 = Markov 1st and 2nd order probabilities.
- R²(40d) = log-trend R² (1 = clean trend, 0 = random).
- Hurst (>0.5) = trending tendency.
- IBS = intraday bar position of close (smaller is better).
- RSI2 = short-term RSI (smaller is better).
- Overhead (≤+1 ATR) = number of prior swing-highs within +1 ATR overhead (smaller is better).
- Weekly Bull = weekly EMA(10) > EMA(20).
- M-FibBonus / KeyLvlBonus = extra score from nearby Fib/key levels.
- RVOL20 = relative 20-day volume.
- ATR% = ATR / Close.

TRADING PLAN (compact)
1) Buy only if Weekly Bull = True and Edge v6 ≥ 30.
2) Prefer setups with RSI2 ≤ 20 and IBS ≤ 0.40 (dips in uptrend).
3) Require Overhead ≤ 2, ATR% 1–4%, RVOL20 ≥ 0.9.
4) Bonus if near M-Fib/KeyLvl (≤0.35 ATR) and NR7+Inside setup.
5) Sell/trim when RSI2 ≥ 90 or R² breaks down and Hurst < 0.45.
